### [59] [Trusted Weights, Treacherous Optimizations? Optimization-Triggered Backdoor Attacks on LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20641v1)
*Yifei Wang,Tianlin Li,Xiaohan Zhang,Yida Yang,Xiaoyu Zhang,Li Pan*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 揭示编译优化可触发后门攻击，对agent安全有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 首次发现LLM编译优化的数值副作用可被利用植入后门，提出两种优化触发攻击策略，在四个模型上平均攻击成功率90%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM编译优化假设语义等价，但数值副作用可能被恶意利用，形成隐蔽后门，威胁模型安全性。

Method: 提出统一优化触发攻击框架，包含两种策略：一是仅编译时翻转特定输入预测；二是使用通用触发器在编译时劫持任意输入，无需修改编译器或硬件。

Result: 在四个开源LLM和四个任务上平均攻击成功率90%，干净准确率几乎100%，且绕过标准安全评估。

Conclusion: 揭示了LLM编译优化与安全性的新攻击面，并探讨了实用防御措施。

中文摘要：推理优化是部署大规模语言模型的关键技术。编译是LLM最广泛采用的优化技术。虽然编译假设原始图和编译后的图在语义上等价，但我们首次发现其数值副作用可被恶意利用，在LLM中植入隐蔽后门。我们提出一个统一的优化触发攻击框架，包含两种互补策略。无需对编译器或硬件做任何修改，一种策略仅在模型被编译时翻转对特定输入的预测，而另一种策略使用通用触发器，在未编译执行下保持休眠，但一旦应用编译优化则劫持任意输入。两种攻击均能绕过未编译时运行的标准安全评估。我们实验证明，这些优化触发后门在四个主流开源LLM和四个任务上平均攻击成功率达90%，而干净准确率在所有设置下几乎保持100%。我们的发现揭示了LLM部署流程中优化与安全性交叉的新攻击面，并研究了实际防御措施以缓解此威胁。

Original abstract: Inference optimization is a vital technique for deploying LLMs at scale. Compilation is the most widely adopted optimization technique for LLMs. While it assumes semantic equivalence between the original and compiled graphs, we first uncover its numerical side effects can be maliciously exploited to implant stealthy backdoors in LLMs. We propose a unified optimization-triggered attack framework comprising two complementary strategies. Without any modification to the compiler or hardware, one strategy flips predictions for specific inputs only when the model is compiled, while the other uses a universal trigger that remains dormant under uncompiled execution but hijacks arbitrary inputs once compilation optimization is applied. Both attacks bypass standard safety evaluations run without compilation. We empirically demonstrate that these optimization-triggered backdoors achieve attack success rates averaging 90% across four mainstream open-source LLMs and four tasks, while clean accuracy is preserved at nearly 100% under all settings. Our findings reveal a novel attack surface at the intersection of optimization and security in the LLM deployment pipeline, and we investigate practical defenses to mitigate this threat.

</details>


### [60] [Heartbeat-Bound Hierarchical Credentials: Cryptographic Revocation for AI Agent Swarms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20704v1)
*Saurabh Deochake*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: AI agent swarm的凭证撤销协议，增强agent安全控制。

TL;DR: HBHC协议通过心跳绑定凭据，在无网络连接下实现快速撤销，极大缩短僵尸窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有凭据撤销机制依赖网络连接，导致撤销延迟大，存在僵尸代理安全隐患。

Method: 提出Heartbeat-Bound Hierarchical Credentials (HBHC)，将凭据有效性绑定到周期性父级心跳，验证者仅需本地公钥和时钟。

Result: 僵尸窗口减少90倍，Rust认证0.26ms，并发18k+验证/秒，工具调用开销0.71%，零撤销后调用。

Conclusion: HBHC有效解决了自主AI代理场景下的撤销延迟问题，提供了安全高效的层次化凭据管理。

中文摘要：自主AI代理在生成子代理群时造成了一个安全缺口：现有的凭据撤销机制，如OAuth 2.0内省、OCSP和W3C状态列表，需要网络连接到中心权威，这使得“僵尸代理”能够在操作者关闭后继续执行特权操作数分钟到数小时。我们提出了心跳绑定层次凭据（HBHC），一种将凭据有效性绑定到周期性父级活跃证明的密码学协议。验证者仅使用缓存的公钥和本地时钟来强制新鲜度；无需网络往返。当心跳生成停止时，所有后代凭据会在一个确定性有界窗口W_z内变得不可用，该窗口满足W_z ≤ W_max + Δ_h + ε，条件为时钟偏差有界且父级密钥保存在安全飞地中。在协议层和真实LLM支持的代理群（GPT-4o-mini）上的评估显示，与OAuth 2.0相比，僵尸窗口减少了90倍，Rust中完全认证仅需0.26毫秒，并发HTTP负载下每秒可进行超过18,000次验证，且从10到10,000个代理的每验证延迟保持稳定。真实代理实验显示，工具调用的端到端开销为0.71%，在绕过应用层防护的即时注入下，撤销后零次工具调用，并且跨49代理的四级层次结构实现了在理论界限内的级联撤销。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents that spawn sub-agent swarms create a safety gap: existing credential revocation mechanisms, OAuth~2.0 introspection, OCSP, and W3C Status Lists, require network connectivity to a central authority, leaving ``zombie agents'' executing privileged operations for minutes to hours after operator shutdown. We present Heartbeat-Bound Hierarchical Credentials (HBHC), a cryptographic protocol that binds credential validity to periodic parent liveness proofs. Verifiers enforce freshness using only a cached public key and local clock; no network round-trip is required. When heartbeat generation ceases, all descendant credentials become unusable within a deterministically bounded window $W_z \le W_{\max} + Δ_h + ε$, conditional on bounded clock skew and parent keys held in secure enclaves. Evaluation at the protocol layer and with real LLM-backed agent swarms (GPT-4o-mini) demonstrates a 90$\times$ reduction in the zombie window over OAuth~2.0, 0.26~ms full authentication in Rust, 18,000+ verifications per second under concurrent HTTP load, and stable per-verification latency from 10 to 10,000 agents. Real-agent experiments show 0.71\% end-to-end overhead on tool calls, zero post-revocation tool calls under prompt injection that bypasses application-layer guardrails, and cascading revocation across a 49-agent four-level hierarchy within the theoretical bound.

</details>


### [61] [An Application-Layer Multi-Modal Covert-Channel Reference Monitor for LLM Agent Egress](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20734v1)
*Alfredo Metere*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent出口安全参考监视器，直接涉及agent安全与控制。

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM代理通过隐蔽通道泄露数据的问题，提出了一个出站参考监控器，包含文本流水线、媒体扰乱器和对抗性残余容量测量，将大部分通道的残余容量降至零，并在一不可破坏通道上达到规定界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有目的地白名单和内容扫描器无法检测基于载荷的隐蔽通道，因此需要一种新方法识别并阻止LLM代理的数据泄露。

Method: 提出了一个包含三个部分的监控器：(i) 文本流水线通过容量缩减阶段和漏桶账本限制通道； (ii) 媒体扰乱器结合启动时密码学证明，区分合法媒体与携带数据的载体； (iii) 使用对抗性编码器集成测量残余容量，并驱动其至零或规定界限。

Result: 参考实现在所有可破坏通道上将残余容量降至零，在不可破坏的每图像平均亮度通道上达到规定的有界容量。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效防止LLM代理通过多种隐蔽通道泄露数据，但某些通道（如平均亮度）的残余容量无法完全消除，只能限制在可接受范围内。

中文摘要：一个发送消息的大型语言模型(LLM)代理可能会在消息内部泄露数据。目的地白名单和内容扫描器不会检查一个原本良性的载荷本身是否是一个隐蔽通道：被攻陷的代理在零宽字符、同形异义词、空白符、base64、JSON键排序、消息时序或大小中编码比特——以及在二进制出站中，在最低有效位(LSB)像素平面、每幅图像的平均亮度、图像间序列置换、超声波音调或可听频段的声化数据中编码。我们的出站参考监控器有三个贡献。(i) 一个包含十个容量缩减阶段的文本流水线、一个每接收器的漏桶容量账本，以及一个从第一天起就强制执行无损阶段的分阶段姿态。(ii) 两个媒体扰乱器（一个傅里叶域音频限带器和一个红绿蓝(RGB)图像位深度和平均亮度分桶器），由启动时的密码学合法性证明门控：审计员在启动时发布受信任的Ed25519密钥和{种类, 数据类别}对；只有具有授权类别的验证签名的载荷才被豁免。该证明绕开了在真实媒体与作为载体的声化或栅格化数据之间进行基于内容的难以区分的鉴别；未签名的媒体默认受到怀疑；一个内容寻址的规范化器关闭了图像间置换通道。(iii) 残余容量是嵌入和恢复比特之间的Miller-Madow校正互信息（当被破坏时为零），由一个包含十五个工作编码器的对抗集成体在文本、图像和音频上进行测量。参考实现将每个可破坏通道的残余容量降至零，并在一个（每幅图像的平均亮度）通道上达到规定的界限，该通道在不破坏图像的情况下无法被破坏。

Original abstract: A large language model (LLM) agent that sends messages can leak data inside them. Destination allowlists and content scanners do not police whether an otherwise-benign payload is itself a covert channel: a compromised agent encodes bits in zero-width characters, homoglyphs, whitespace, base64, JavaScript Object Notation (JSON) key ordering, message timing or size -- and, in binary egress, in least-significant-bit (LSB) pixel planes, per-image mean luminance, inter-image sequence permutation, ultrasonic tones, or audible-band sonified data. Our egress reference monitor has three contributions. (i) A text pipeline of ten capacity-reducing stages, a per-sink leaky-bucket capacity ledger, and a staged posture that enforces lossless stages from day one. (ii) Two media scramblers (a Fourier-domain audio band-limiter and a red-green-blue (RGB) image bit-depth and mean-luminance bucketer) gated by a boot-time cryptographic legitimacy attestation: an auditor publishes at boot the trusted Ed25519 keys and {kind, data-class} pairs; only payloads with a verifying signature for an authorized class are exempt. The attestation sidesteps the intractable content-based discrimination between real media and data sonified or rasterized as a carrier; unsigned media is suspect by default; a content-addressed canonicalizer closes the inter-image permutation channel. (iii) Residual capacity is the Miller--Madow corrected mutual information between embedded and recovered bits (zero when destroyed), measured by an adversarial ensemble of fifteen working encoders across text, image and audio. The reference implementation drives residual capacity to zero on every destroyable channel and to a stated bound on the one (per-image mean luminance) that cannot be destroyed without ruining the image.

</details>


### [62] [GenAI-Driven Threat Detection with Microsoft Security Copilot](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20896v2)
*Scott Freitas,Amir Gharib*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 安全agent含规划-执行循环与动态警报，其agent工作流设计可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: DTDA是一个自适应代理，通过连续调查安全事件生成可解释检测，在线评估精确率80.1%，离线F1 0.78。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全分析师需不断更新知识以应对复杂攻击，处于被动姿态。

Method: DTDA结合统一活动时间线、版本化LLM提示合约、规划器-执行器调查循环和动态警报生成。

Result: 在线评估精确率80.1%，新警报率15%；离线F1 0.78；中位处理时间28分钟，成本2.04美元，故障率0.38%。

Conclusion: 自主代理可在生产规模识别遗漏恶意活动。

中文摘要：应对当今日益复杂的网络攻击，需要安全分析师不断将不断演变的攻击者战术转化为检测逻辑。这使防御者处于被动姿态，需要在日益碎片化的安全环境中不断更新专业知识。我们介绍了动态威胁检测代理（DTDA），一种始终在线的自适应代理，持续调查Microsoft Defender中的安全事件，以发现隐藏的威胁，并在发现攻击故事缺口时生成可解释的检测。DTDA结合了：（1）统一的活动时间线，涵盖警报、事件、用户和实体行为分析以及威胁情报；（2）版本化的LLM提示合约，包括模式验证、接地要求、有限重试和故障关闭抑制；（3）规划器-执行器调查循环，生成针对特定攻击的假设并收集支持和反驳证据；（4）动态警报生成，包含上下文相关的标题、严重性、MITRE映射、修复指导、涉及实体和自然语言攻击描述。DTDA集成到Microsoft Security Copilot中，并部署在数以万计的Defender客户中，在行业规模下持续运行。在120天的在线评估中，DTDA根据客户反馈实现了80.1%的精确率，同时为大约15%的调查事件生成了新警报。在离线评估中，DTDA使用GPT-5.4以0.78的F1分数恢复了隐藏的恶意活动，比GPT-4.1提高了0.12 F1，比基线提高了0.26 F1。在操作上，DTDA处理单个事件调查的中位端到端时间为28分钟，中位令牌成本为2.04美元，作业级故障率为0.38%。这些结果表明，自主代理可以在生产规模上识别遗漏的恶意活动。

Original abstract: Defending against today's increasingly sophisticated cyberattacks requires security analysts to continuously translate evolving attacker tradecraft into detection logic. This places defenders in a reactive posture, requiring constantly updated expertise across an increasingly fragmented security landscape. We introduce the Dynamic Threat Detection Agent (DTDA), an always-on adaptive agent that continuously investigates security incidents across Microsoft Defender to uncover hidden threats and generate explainable detections when attack-story gaps are found. DTDA combines: (1) a unified activity timeline spanning alerts, events, user and entity behavior analytics, and threat intelligence; (2) versioned LLM prompt contracts with schema validation, grounding requirements, bounded retries, and fail-closed suppression; (3) a planner-executor investigation loop that generates attack-specific hypotheses and gathers supporting and refuting evidence; and (4) dynamic alert generation with a context-relevant title, severity, MITRE mappings, remediation guidance, implicated entities, and natural-language attack description. Integrated into Microsoft Security Copilot and deployed across tens of thousands of Defender customers, DTDA operates continuously at industry scale. In a 120-day online evaluation, DTDA achieves 80.1% precision from customer feedback while generating novel alerts for approximately 15% of investigated incidents. In offline evaluation, DTDA recovers hidden malicious activity with 0.78 F1 using GPT-5.4, improving over GPT-4.1 by 0.12 F1 and outperforming the baseline by 0.26 F1 points. Operationally, DTDA processes single-incident investigations end-to-end in a median of 28 minutes at a median token cost of USD 2.04, with a 0.38% job-level failure rate. These results demonstrate that autonomous agents can identify missed malicious activity at a production scale.

### [63] [Detecting Trojaned DNNs via Spectral Regression Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21146v1)
*Samuele Pasini,Jinhan Kim,Paolo Tonella*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: MIST通过分析模型微调中预激活谱的变化来检测木马，无需触发器知识，在单次更新后即实现高精度检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代DNN反复微调以融入新数据，但更新数据可能不可信，存在植入后门木马的风险。现有检测方法通常需要重建触发器，具有强假设。

Method: MIST使用预激活谱表征良性模型演进，将木马检测视为回归问题：比较模型更新后的谱偏差与参考谱，若不一致则判定为恶意更新。

Result: 在四个数据集和八种攻击下，谱距离可靠区分木马更新与干净微调，优于最先进方法，无需中毒数据或触发器知识，多步良性演进下性能退化有界。

Conclusion: 谱演变为检测恶意模型更新提供了稳定且假设较少的信号，有效且鲁棒。

中文摘要：现代DNN被反复微调以融入新数据和功能。这种演进工作流在更新数据不能完全信任时引入了安全风险，因为对手可能在微调期间植入木马。我们提出MIST，一种通过分析模型内部表示在微调期间如何变化来进行木马检测的方法。MIST不试图重建触发器条件，而是使用预激活谱来表征良性模型演进，并标记那些谱偏差与此参考不一致的更新。这种框架将木马检测视为模型更新上的回归问题。在四个数据集和八种木马攻击上的实证评估表明，谱距离能够可靠地区分被植入木马的更新和干净微调。MIST在单次更新后即优于最先进的检测精度，无需任何关于中毒数据或触发器的知识，并且在多步良性演进下仍然有效，具有优雅且有界的退化。这些结果表明，谱演变为检测恶意模型更新提供了一种稳定且假设较少的信号。

Original abstract: Modern DNNs are repeatedly fine-tuned to incorporate new data and functionality. This evolutionary workflow introduces a security risk when updated data cannot be fully trusted, as adversaries may implant Trojans during fine-tuning. We present MIST, a Trojan detection approach that analyzes how a model's internal representations change during fine-tuning. Rather than attempting to reconstruct trigger conditions, MIST characterizes benign model evolution using pre-activation spectra and flags updates whose spectral deviations are inconsistent with this reference. This framing treats Trojan detection as a regression problem over model updates. An empirical evaluation across four datasets and eight Trojan attacks shows that spectral distances reliably distinguish Trojaned updates from clean fine-tuning. MIST outperforms state-of-the-art detection accuracy after a single update, without requiring any knowledge about the poisoned data or the trigger, and remains effective under multi-step benign evolution, with graceful and bounded degradation. These results indicate that spectral evolution provides a stable and assumption-light signal for detecting malicious model updates.

### [64] [ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY: A Cross-Build Binary Dataset with Temporal Coverage](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21615v1)
*Chang Liu,Noah Fleischmann,Nicolò Altamura,Edward Raff,James Holt,Kristopher Micinski*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY，一个包含73,610个二进制文件的统一数据库，整合了跨编译器、跨版本和CVE信息，并通过三个实验证明了其在二进制分析中的价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有二进制语料库只覆盖跨构建或CVE标签等单一维度，缺乏将跨构建多样性、历史版本和漏洞标签结合的可查询结构，限制了二进制分析的研究。

Method: 构建ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY，包含来自248个开源项目的73,610个二进制文件，使用GCC、Clang和MSVC在Linux和Windows上以多优化级别编译，覆盖多年历史。每个二进制与其源代码、函数、调试信息、变体构建、历史版本和易受攻击函数关联。通过三个分析验证：LLM基准测试、嵌入和模糊哈希比较、贝叶斯回归。

Result: 三个分析结果表明：LLM在二进制漏洞推理中易受构建特定工件影响；MalConv、jTrans和TLSH对同包版本的聚类能力不同；二进制相似性主要由时间距离和文件更改解释。

Conclusion: ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY为二进制分析提供了丰富的多维度数据，能够支持漏洞研究、二进制相似性分析和LLM评估等多种任务，具有重要价值。

中文摘要：现有的二进制语料库通常只捕获二进制变化的一个或两个轴：它们要么在缺少时间轴的情况下提供跨编译器构建，要么为单一构建二进制文件提供CVE标签。没有一种方法能将跨构建多样性、跨版本历史和CVE标签组合成可查询的结构。我们提出了ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY，它将这些维度整合到一个统一的框架中，其中每个二进制的编译上下文、源代码、易受攻击的函数和包版本都作为第一类元数据存储。ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY包含73,610个二进制文件，涵盖248个开源项目，在GCC、Clang和MSVC上以多种优化级别在Linux和Windows上编译，并具有多年的历史构建。每个二进制文件都索引在一个数据库中，该数据库将其链接到其源代码、函数、调试信息、变体构建、历史版本和易受攻击的函数。三个分析证明了这种结构的价值：(1) 一个三阶段的LLM基准测试（识别、策略引导检测和跨构建迁移），测试LLM是否推理二进制漏洞还是对构建特定工件进行模式匹配；(2) MalConv嵌入、jTrans函数嵌入和TLSH模糊哈希的比较，量化了相同包版本在每个空间中的聚类情况；(3) 贝叶斯回归将二进制相似性分解为时间距离、文件更改和提交的贡献。

Original abstract: Existing binary corpora typically capture only one or two axes of binary variation: they either provide cross-compiler builds without a temporal axis, or CVE labels for single-build binaries. None combine cross-build diversity, cross-version history, and CVE labels into a queryable structure. We present ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY, which consolidates these dimensions into a unified framework where every binary's compilation context, source code, vulnerable functions, and package version are stored as first-class metadata.
  ASSEMBLAGE-DEEPHISTORY comprises 73,610 binaries spanning 248 open-source projects, compiled across GCC, Clang, and MSVC at multiple optimization levels on Linux and Windows, with multi-year historical builds. Each binary is indexed in a database that links it to its source code, functions, debug info, variant builds, historical versions, and vulnerable functions. Three analyses demonstrate this structure's value: (1) a three-stage LLM benchmark (recognition, strategy-guided detection, and cross-build transfer) to test whether LLMs reason about binary vulnerabilities or pattern-match on build-specific artifacts; (2) a comparison of MalConv embeddings, jTrans function embeddings, and TLSH fuzzy hashes quantifying how same-package versions cluster in each space; and (3) a Bayesian regression decomposing binary similarity into contributions from temporal distance, file changes, and commits.

</details>


### [65] [PocketAgents: A Manifest-Driven Library of Autonomous Defense Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21694v1)
*Sidnei Barbieri,Ágney Lopes Roth Ferraz,Lourenço Alves Pereira Júnior*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出manifest驱动的自主防御agent架构，含typed reports和runtime，对通用agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出PocketAgents，一个基于清单的自主防御代理库，通过类型化边界使LLM驱动的防御可测量、可扩展和可归因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连接LLM到防御执行需要超越简单询问，需要决定输出影响、拒绝和记录失败的方式。

Method: 设计PocketAgents库，每个代理由清单、提示和运行时上下文组成，共享运行时只接受类型化报告；在Perry竞技场和网络欺骗测试床上进行实验。

Result: 18个闭环试验中，13次产生验证的网络阻止动作，4次模式验证失败，1次无动作决策。

Conclusion: 类型化边界使LLM驱动防御可测量、可扩展和可归因。

中文摘要：将大型语言模型（LLM）连接到防御执行不仅仅需要询问模型是否正在发生攻击。防御者必须决定哪些模型输出可能改变系统状态，哪些输出必须被拒绝，以及应如何记录失败。我们提出PocketAgents，一个基于清单的自主防御代理库。每个代理作为三个数据文件安装：一个清单、一个提示词和一个运行时上下文。共享运行时赋予代理有限的遥测访问权限，并且只接受其请求的动作出现在清单中的类型化报告。我们在网络竞技场（Perry）——一个网络欺骗测试床之上实现了PocketAgents，并在一个受DarkSide启发的小型企业拓扑攻击的18次闭环试验中评估了两个代理：命令与控制代理以及外泄代理。其中13次试验产生了经过验证的网络阻止动作并遏制了攻击；4次试验未能通过模式验证；1次试验产生了有效的“不采取行动”决策。实验表明，类型化边界使得LLM驱动的防御变得可测量、可扩展且可归因。

Original abstract: Connecting large language models (LLMs) to defensive enforcement requires more than asking a model whether an attack is happening. A defender must decide which model outputs may change the system state, which outputs must be rejected, and how failures should be recorded. We present PocketAgents, a manifest-driven library of autonomous defense agents. Each agent is installed as three data files: a manifest, a prompt, and a runtime context. The shared runtime gives the agent bounded telemetry access and accepts only typed reports whose requested action appears in the manifest. We implemented PocketAgents on top of a cyber arena (Perry), a cyber-deception testbed, and evaluated two agents, Command and Control and Exfiltration, in 18 closed-loop trials of a DarkSide-inspired attack on a small enterprise topology. Thirteen trials produced validated network-block actions and contained the attack; four failed schema validation; one produced a valid no-action decision. The experiments show that a typed boundary makes LLM-driven defense measurable, extensible, and attributable.

### [66] [FuzzingBrain V2: A Multi-Agent LLM System for Automated Vulnerability Discovery and Reproduction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21779v1)
*Ze Sheng,Zhicheng Chen,Qingxiao Xu,Kewen Zhu,Jeff Huang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: FuzzingBrain V2是一个多智能体系统，通过基于OSS-Fuzz的全自动分析、Suspicious Point定位、逻辑驱动分层函数分析和MCP工具，在AIxCC数据集上达到90%检测率，并在真实项目中发现了29个零日漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件漏洞威胁严重，现有LLM漏洞检测方法存在高误报率、粒度不优（函数级忽略细节、行级缺乏上下文）以及难以处理复杂跨函数依赖和触发条件的问题。

Method: 四个关键贡献：1) 基于OSS-Fuzz的自动化分析确保可重现；2) Suspicious Point控制流抽象实现最优粒度定位；3) 逻辑驱动分层函数分析与双层模糊测试增强覆盖；4) MCP静态/动态分析工具结合上下文工程推理复杂漏洞。

Result: 在AIxCC 2025决赛C/C++数据集中检测率达到90%（36/40）；在实际部署中发现29个零日漏洞（12个项目），全部修复，2个获得CVE。

Conclusion: FuzzingBrain V2有效解决了LLM漏洞检测的三大挑战，实现了高检测率和实际漏洞发现能力，证明了多智能体结合自动化分析、粒度优化和复杂推理的有效性。

中文摘要：软件漏洞构成严重的安全威胁，2025年报告了近50,000个CVE。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在自动化漏洞检测方面显示出潜力，但仍存在三个关键挑战。首先，LLM生成的漏洞报告误报率高且缺乏可重复验证。其次，现有的基于LLM的方法在漏洞定位中使用次优粒度：函数级分析在上下文广泛时会忽略漏洞，而行级分析缺乏足够的上下文。第三，现有方法难以推理具有复杂跨函数依赖和触发条件的漏洞。我们提出了FuzzingBrain V2，这是一个多智能体系统，通过四个关键贡献解决了这些差距：（1）基于Google的OSS-Fuzz构建的全自动漏洞分析，确保所有报告的漏洞均可由模糊测试重现；（2）Suspicious Point，一种新颖的基于控制流的抽象，用于在最优粒度下精确定位漏洞；（3）逻辑驱动的分层函数分析，结合双层模糊测试，在资源约束下增强函数覆盖；（4）基于MCP的静态和动态分析工具，结合上下文工程，增强复杂漏洞推理。在AIxCC 2025决赛C/C++数据集上，FuzzingBrain V2实现了90%的检测率（40个漏洞中的36个）。在实际部署中，FuzzingBrain V2在12个开源项目中发现了29个零日漏洞，全部由维护者确认并修复，其中2个已分配CVE ID。

Original abstract: Software vulnerabilities pose critical security threats, with nearly 50,000 CVEs reported in 2025. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise for automated vulnerability detection, three key challenges remain. First, LLM-generated vulnerability reports suffer from high false positive rates and lack
  reproducible verification. Second, existing LLM-based approaches use suboptimal granularities for vulnerability localization: function-level analysis overlooks bugs when context becomes extensive, while line-level analysis lacks sufficient context. Third, existing approaches have difficulty reasoning about
  vulnerabilities with complex cross-function dependencies and triggering conditions.
  We present FuzzingBrain V2, a multi-agent system that addresses these gaps through four key contributions: (1) fully automated vulnerability analysis built on Google's OSS-Fuzz, ensuring all reported vulnerabilities are fuzzer-reproducible; (2) Suspicious Point, a novel control-flow-based abstraction for precise
  vulnerability localization at the optimal granularity; (3) logic-driven hierarchical function analysis with dual-layer fuzzing enhancing function coverage under resource constraints; (4) MCP-based static and dynamic analysis tools with context engineering enhancing complex vulnerability reasoning.
  On the AIxCC 2025 Final Competition C/C++ dataset, FuzzingBrain V2 achieved 90% detection rate (36 of 40 vulnerabilities). In real-world deployment, FuzzingBrain V2 discovered 29 zero-day vulnerabilities across 12 open-source projects, all confirmed and fixed by maintainers, with 2 assigned CVE IDs.

</details>


### [67] [Quality-Assured Fuzz Harness Generation via the Four Principles Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21824v1)
*Ze Sheng,Dmitrijs Trizna,Luigino Camastra,Zhicheng Chen,Qingxiao Xu,Jeff Huang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: QuartetFuzz是一个基于四原则框架的自主测试工具生成系统，通过LLM智能体和生成-检查-修复循环系统性地确保工具正确性，在23个开源项目中发现42个bug（29个确认），并作为审计员识别出53个现有工具违规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化工具生成方法无法系统性地确保工具正确性，导致逻辑错误、API误用和生命周期违规在源代码层面未被检测，LLM驱动的生成使规模成为负担。

Method: 提出四原则框架（逻辑正确性P1、API协议合规性P2、安全边界尊重P3、入口点充分性P4），作为首个具有数学规范和可实施检查的源代码级工具正确性定义，并实现为自主LLM智能体，通过生成-检查-修复循环生成满足P1-P4的工具。

Result: 在23个开源项目中提交42个bug报告，29个被确认（含3个CVE），仅2个被拒绝（4.8% FP率）；生成过程中内置P1/P2检查自动拦截58次工具引起的崩溃；审计70个项目586个现有生产工具，发现53个违规（45个确认，35个修复）；发布含100个标记工具的数据集。

Conclusion: QuartetFuzz能有效提升测试工具正确性，减少误报，可扩展至多语言项目，并作为质量审计工具发现现有工具中的问题。

中文摘要：模糊测试是发现C/C++软件中内存安全漏洞的主要技术，但其有效性取决于模糊测试工具的质量——即连接模糊器和库API的程序。越来越多的工具现可自动生成测试工具，但没有任何工具能系统性地确保所生成工具的正确性：逻辑错误、API误用和生命周期违规在源代码层面未被检测到。随着LLM驱动的生成技术扩展了工具创建规模，不受控制的质量使得规模成为一种负担。我们提出QuartetFuzz，一个自主的测试工具生成系统，在整个生成过程中系统性地提高正确性。其核心是四原则框架——逻辑正确性（P1）、API协议合规性（P2）、安全边界尊重（P3）和入口点充分性（P4）——这是首个具有数学规范和可实施检查的源代码级工具正确性定义。我们在一个自主的LLM智能体中实现了这些原则，该智能体通过生成-检查-修复循环，在开始任何模糊测试之前生成满足P1-P4的工具。该系统部署在涵盖C/C++、Java和JavaScript的23个开源项目上，提交了42个错误报告，其中29个已被上游修复或确认（包括3个CVE），仅2个被拒绝（4.8%假阳性率）。在生成过程中，内置的P1/P2检查自动拦截了58次由工具引起的崩溃，否则这些崩溃将成为误报。作为质量审计员应用于70个项目中586个现有生产工具时，该系统识别出53个违规（45个已确认，35个已修复）。我们发布了一个包含100个标记工具的数据集，用于可重复评估。代码和数据集可在https://github.com/OwenSanzas/QuartetFuzz获取。

Original abstract: Fuzz testing is the dominant technique for finding memory-safety vulnerabilities in C/C++ software, yet its effectiveness hinges on the quality of fuzz harnesses -- the programs that bridge fuzzers and library APIs. A growing body of tools now automate harness generation, but none systematically ensures the correctness of produced harnesses: logic errors, API misuse, and lifecycle violations go undetected at the source level. As LLM-driven generation scales harness creation, uncontrolled quality turns scale into a liability.
  We present QuartetFuzz, an autonomous harness-generation system that systematically improves correctness throughout the generation process. At its core is the Four Principles framework -- Logic Correctness (P1), API Protocol Compliance (P2), Security Boundary Respect (P3), and Entry Point Adequacy (P4) -- the first source-level definition of harness correctness with mathematical specifications and implementable checks. We operationalize these principles in an autonomous LLM agent that produces harnesses satisfying P1-P4 through a generate-check-fix loop before any fuzzing begins.
  Deployed on 23 open-source projects spanning C/C++, Java, and JavaScript, the system submits 42 bug reports, of which 29 are fixed or confirmed upstream (including 3 CVEs) and only 2 are rejected (4.8% FP rate). During generation, the built-in P1/P2 checks automatically intercepted 58 harness-induced crashes that would otherwise have been false positives. Applied as a quality auditor to 586 existing production harnesses across 70 projects, the system identifies 53 violations (45 confirmed, 35 fixed). We release a dataset of 100 labeled harnesses for reproducible evaluation. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/OwenSanzas/QuartetFuzz

</details>

### [68] [MedExpMem: Adapting Experience Memory for Differential Diagnosis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22872v1)
*Qianhan Feng,Zhongzhen Huang,Yakun Zhu,Yannian Gu,Winnie Chiu Wing Chu,Xiaofan Zhang,Qi Dou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出experience memory框架用于医学诊断agent，记忆机制可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: MedExpMem通过记忆诊断失败经验提升VLM鉴别诊断能力，在放射学基准上最高提升7.0%准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前医学VLM缺乏像医生一样从临床实践中积累鉴别诊断经验的能力，参数静态无法进化。

Method: 提出MedExpMem框架，两阶段构建：初始实践暴露知识差距，反思性再诊断细化经验；将代理诊断失败生成成对鉴别笔记，存入经验记忆库，新病例时检索辅助推理。

Result: 在11个亚专业放射学基准上，准确率持续提升，最大7.0%，并验证了经验质量和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: MedExpMem有效解决了参数学习无法覆盖的医学适应需求，通过经验记忆实现诊断能力进化。

中文摘要：经验丰富的医生通过临床实践发展诊断专业知识，不仅获取疾病知识，还能区分易混淆的病症。当前的医学视觉语言模型（VLM）缺乏这种能力——它们的参数编码静态知识，不会在诊断中进化。我们提出了MedExpMem，一种经验记忆框架，使基于VLM的诊断代理能够积累鉴别诊断专业知识。与检索增强生成（检索百科全书式的疾病描述）不同，MedExpMem从代理自身的诊断失败中记忆区分性经验，并将其组织为成对的鉴别笔记，编码关键鉴别因子、可操作的决策规则和推理错误模式。该框架采用两阶段构建过程，模拟医生学习：初始实践暴露知识差距，反思性再诊断完善理解。当面对新病例时，代理检索经验记忆以指导鉴别推理。我们在覆盖11个亚专业的放射学基准上评估了MedExpMem。结果表明，在不同模型和规模上，准确率持续提升，最大提升7.0%。分析实验验证了经验质量和鲁棒性，表明MedExpMem是一种有竞争力的方法，解决了参数学习无法触及的医学适应需求。

Original abstract: Experienced physicians develop diagnostic expertise through clinical practice, acquiring not only disease knowledge but also the ability to differentiate confusable conditions. Current medical vision-language models (VLMs) lack this capability -- their parameters encode static knowledge that does not evolve across diagnostic encounters. We propose MedExpMem, an experience memory framework enabling VLM-based diagnostic agents to accumulate differential diagnosis expertise. Unlike retrieval-augmented generation, which retrieves encyclopedic disease descriptions, MedExpMem memorizes discriminative experience derived from the agent's own diagnostic failures and organizes them as pairwise differential notes encoding key discriminators, actionable decision rules and reasoning error patterns. The framework adopts a two-phase construction process mirroring physician learning: initial practice exposes knowledge gaps, and reflective re-diagnosis refines understanding. When encountering new cases, the agent retrieves experience memory to guide differential reasoning. We evaluate MedExpMem on a radiology benchmark spanning 11 subspecialties. Results demonstrate consistent accuracy improvements, maximum 7.0%, across diverse models and scales. Analytical experiments validate experience quality and robustness, demonstrating MedExpMem as a competitive method addresses medical adaptation needs beyond the reach of parameteric learning.

</details>


### [69] [AVSD: Adaptive-View Self-Distillation by Balancing Consensus and Teacher-Specific Privileged Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20643v1)
*Duy Nguyen,Hanqi Xiao,Archiki Prasad,Zaid Khan,Anirban Das,Austin Zhang,Sambit Sahu,Hyunji Lee,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多视图自蒸馏训练方法，在代码生成任务上验证，可迁移至agent训练。

TL;DR: AVSD通过分离跨视图共识和视图特定残差信号，实现了利用多个特权信息视图的自蒸馏，在数学和代码生成任务上优于单视图基线和GRPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自蒸馏中教师依赖视图特定信息而学生无法访问，且最佳特权信息类型因任务而异，单一视图难以选择，因此需要一种能利用多个视图并处理不对称性的方法。

Method: AVSD（自适应视图自蒸馏）方法，通过分离稳定的跨视图共识信号（提供更新方向）和视图特定残差信号（调整更新幅度），仅在残差信号与共识方向一致且成比例时选择性添加，从而结合多个特权信息视图。

Result: 在数学竞赛基准上，AVSD在Qwen3-8B和Qwen3-4B上分别取得3.1%和2.2%的Avg@8增益；在代码生成基准上，AVSD平均比单视图基线高2.4%。

Conclusion: AVSD通过多视图自蒸馏有效解决了教师-学生不对称和视图选择问题，在多种任务上显著提升了性能。

中文摘要：自蒸馏使语言模型能够通过使用同一模型同时作为学生和教师，从自身轨迹中进行在策略学习，其中教师以学生无法获得的特权信息为条件。这种信息可以以不同类型或视图的形式出现，例如解决方案、演示、反馈或最终答案。这种设置提供了密集的令牌级反馈，无需依赖外部模型，但造成了一个根本性的不对称：教师可能依赖于学生在推理时无法访问的视图特定信息。此外，最佳的特权信息类型通常依赖于任务，使得选择单一的教师视图变得困难。在这项工作中，我们通过引入AVSD（自适应视图自蒸馏）来共同解决这两个挑战，这是一种具有多个特权信息视图的自蒸馏新方法，通过将稳定的跨视图共识与视图特定残差信号分离来重建令牌级监督。AVSD识别跨视图共享的共识信号，该信号提供可靠的更新方向，然后选择性地添加视图特定残差信号，当该信号与共识方向一致且与共识信号成比例时，调整更新幅度。在数学竞赛基准（AIME24、AIME25和HMMT25）上的实验表明，AVSD始终优于单视图自蒸馏基线和GRPO，在Qwen3-8B和Qwen3-4B上分别比最强基线平均获得3.1%和2.2%的Avg@8增益。此外，在使用Qwen3-8B的代码生成基准（Codeforces、LiveCodeBench v6）上，AVSD平均比单视图自蒸馏基线高出2.4%。

Original abstract: Self-distillation enables language models to learn on-policy from their own trajectories by using the same model as both student and teacher, with the teacher being conditioned on privileged information unavailable to the student. Such information can come in different types or views, such as solutions, demonstrations, feedback, or final answers. This setup provides dense token-level feedback without relying on a separate external model, but creates a fundamental asymmetry: the teacher may rely on view-specific information that the student cannot access at inference time. Moreover, the best type of privileged information is often task-dependent, making it difficult to choose a single teacher view. In this work, we address both these challenges jointly by introducing AVSD (Adaptive-View Self-Distillation), a novel method of self-distillation with multiple privileged-information views, which reconstructs token-level supervision by separating stable cross-view consensus from view-specific residual signals. AVSD identifies the consensus signal shared across views, which provides a reliable update direction, and then selectively adds the view-specific residual signal to adjust the update magnitude when it both aligns with the consensus direction and remains proportionate to the consensus signal. Experiments on math competition benchmarks (AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25) show that AVSD consistently outperforms both single-view self-distillation baselines and GRPO, achieving average Avg@8 gains of 3.1% and 2.2% over the strongest baselines on Qwen3-8B and Qwen3-4B, respectively. Moreover, on code-generation benchmarks (Codeforces, LiveCodeBench v6) using Qwen3-8B, AVSD outperforms the single-view self-distillation baseline by 2.4% on average.

</details>


### [70] [When Do LLMs Reason? A Dynamical Systems View via Entropy Phase Transitions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22873v2)
*Wei Xia,Haoqing Wang,Zhi-Hong Deng,Yehui Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于熵动态选择推理策略，可提升agent推理效率与token节省。

TL;DR: 提出EDRM框架，通过早期解码熵动态自适应选择推理策略，在多个基准上实现token减少和准确率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CoT推理在事实性和开放式任务上收益有限且token消耗大，需要判断何时显式推理真正有益。

Method: 基于早期解码熵动力学构建轻量级流形表示，无需训练即可自适应选择推理策略（如CoT或直接回答）。

Result: 在15个基准和4种LLM上，数据集级token减少41-55%且准确率提升，实例级token节省27-45%且准确率提升4.7%。

Conclusion: 推理应选择性调用而非默认使用，熵驱动的解码控制能实现高效自适应的LLM推理。

中文摘要：链式思维（CoT）推理已成为增强LLM能力的默认策略，但其应用引发了一个基本问题：显式推理何时真正有益？实证证据揭示了一个显著悖论：CoT在事实性和开放式任务上通常提供边际甚至负增益，同时成倍增加token消耗。在这项工作中，我们表明LLM推理不是任务或模型的静态属性，而是在生成过程中出现的动态解码状态。通过系统分析，我们发现早期熵动力学为这种状态提供了可靠信号：从CoT中受益的任务表现出一致的熵减少，而其他任务则表现出不稳定或增加的模式。这种行为可以被解释为从高熵探索阶段到低熵结构推理阶段的相变式转变。基于这些见解，我们提出了EDRM（基于熵动力学的推理流形），一个轻量级且无需训练的推理框架，利用早期解码熵自适应选择推理策略。EDRM将熵轨迹嵌入到紧凑且可解释的流形表示中，实现零样本部署和细粒度实例级适应。在15个基准测试和4种不同规模和架构的LLM上，EDRM始终优于静态基线。在数据集层面，EDRM实现了41-55%的token减少，同时仅用50个校准样本就提高了准确性。在实例层面，它进一步将准确率提高了高达4.7%，同时保持了27-45%的token节省。这些结果表明，推理应该被有选择地调用而非默认使用，并证明了熵驱动的解码控制对于高效且自适应的LLM推理的有效性。

Original abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has become the default strategy for enhancing LLM capabilities, yet its application raises a fundamental question: when is explicit reasoning actually beneficial? Empirical evidence reveals a striking paradox: CoT often provides marginal or even negative gains on factual and open-ended tasks while multiplying token consumption. In this work, we show that LLM reasoning is not a static property of tasks or models, but a \emph{dynamic decoding state} that emerges during generation. Through systematic analysis, we find early-stage entropy dynamics provide a reliable signal of this state: tasks benefiting from CoT exhibit consistent entropy reduction, while others display unstable or increasing patterns. This behavior can be interpreted as a phase-transition-like shift from a high-entropy exploratory regime to a low-entropy structured reasoning regime. Based on these insights, we propose \textbf{EDRM} (Entropy Dynamics-based Reasoning Manifold), a lightweight and training-free routing framework that leverages early decoding entropy to adaptively select inference strategies. EDRM embeds entropy trajectories into a compact and interpretable manifold representation, enabling both zero-shot deployment and fine-grained instance-level adaptation. Across 15 benchmarks and 4 LLMs of varying scales and architectures, EDRM consistently outperforms static baselines. At the dataset level, EDRM achieves \textbf{41--55\%} token reduction while improving accuracy with as few as 50 calibration samples. At the instance level, it further improves accuracy by up to \textbf{4.7\%} while maintaining \textbf{27--45\%} token savings. These results suggest that reasoning should be invoked selectively rather than by default, and demonstrate the effectiveness of entropy-driven decoding control for efficient and adaptive LLM inference.

</details>


### [71] [REFLECTOR: Internalizing Step-wise Reflection against Indirect Jailbreak](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20654v2)
*Jiachen Ma,Jiawen Zhang,Xiangtian Li,Bo Zou,Chaochao Lu,Chao Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 内化自反思框架防御越狱，self-reflection机制可迁移至coding agent鲁棒性。

TL;DR: 提出Reflector框架，通过内化自我反思提升LLM对越狱攻击的防御能力，实现超过90%防御成功率并增强通用实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM易受复杂多步越狱攻击，传统表面安全对齐不足以应对利用内部生成过程的攻击。

Method: 两阶段框架：阶段一利用教师引导生成反思数据进行监督微调建立结构化反思模式；阶段二使用结果驱动和奖励有效性监督的强化学习培养自主自我反思能力。

Result: 防御成功率超过90%对抗复杂间接攻击；GSM8K提升5.85%，知识密集型基准性能提升；泛化能力强。

Conclusion: 通过内化轨迹级安全性有效克服表面对齐限制，无需显著计算开销，提供高效可扩展的安全LLM解决方案。

中文摘要：尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）展示了卓越的能力，但它们仍然容易受到复杂的多步越狱攻击，这些攻击通过利用内部生成过程来规避传统的表面安全对齐。为了解决这些漏洞，我们提出了Reflector，一个原则性的两阶段框架，将自我反思内化到生成轨迹中。Reflector首先利用教师引导生成高质量反思数据用于监督微调（SFT），建立结构化的反思模式。随后，它使用带有结果驱动和奖励有效性监督的强化学习（RL）来培养稳健、自主的自我反思能力。实验结果表明，Reflector在对抗复杂间接攻击时实现了超过90%的防御成功率（DSR），同时在不同威胁场景下具有稳健的泛化能力。值得注意的是，该框架增强了任务特定和通用实用性，在GSM8K上获得了5.85%的提升，并在知识密集型基准测试上也有所改进。通过内化轨迹级安全性，Reflector克服了表面对齐的基本限制，而无需显著的计算开销，为开发安全且能力强大的LLMs提供了一种高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable capabilities, they remain susceptible to sophisticated, multi-step jailbreak attacks that circumvent conventional surface-level safety alignment by exploiting the internal generation process. To address these vulnerabilities, we propose Reflector, a principled two-stage framework that internalizes self-reflection within the generation trajectory. Reflector first leverages teacher-guided generation to produce high-quality reflection data for supervised fine-tuning (SFT), establishing structured reflection patterns. It subsequently uses Reinforcement Learning (RL) with outcome-driven and reward-validity supervision to instill robust, autonomous self-reflection capabilities. Empirical results show that Reflector achieves Defense Success Rates (DSR) exceeding 90% against complex indirect attacks while generalizing robustly across diverse threat scenarios. Notably, the framework enhances both task-specific and general utility, yielding a 5.85% gain on GSM8K alongside improved performance on knowledge-intensive benchmarks. By internalizing trajectory-level safety, Reflector overcomes the fundamental limitations of surface alignment without significant computational overhead, offering an efficient and scalable solution for the development of safe and capable LLMs.

</details>


### [72] [Hack-Verifiable Environments: Towards Evaluating Reward Hacking at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20744v1)
*Amit Roth,Ankur Samanta,Matan Halevy,Yoav Levine,Yonathan Efroni*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出评估reward hacking的可验证环境，可迁移至coding agent安全评测

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的评估范式，通过将可检测的奖励黑客机会嵌入环境来可靠测量智能体的奖励黑客行为，并基于TextArena构建了测试平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏大规模可靠测量奖励黑客行为的手段，需要一种可验证的自动化评估方式。

Method: 设计可嵌入环境的奖励黑客机会，使智能体对漏洞的利用可验证，并在TextArena环境中实例化，形成Hack-Verifiable TextArena测试床。

Result: 利用该基准分析了多种语言模型在不同环境中的奖励黑客行为。

Conclusion: 通过嵌入可验证的奖励黑客机会，能够可靠地检测和测量智能体的奖励黑客行为，为对齐研究提供有效工具。

中文摘要：将自主智能体与人类意图对齐仍然是现代人工智能中的核心挑战。这一挑战的一个关键表现是奖励黑客行为，即智能体在评估信号下看似成功，却违背了预期目标。奖励黑客行为已在多种场景中被观察到，但大规模可靠测量其程度的方法仍然缺乏。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种新的评估范式来测量奖励黑客行为。以往研究主要通过事后分析智能体轨迹来研究该行为，而我们则将可检测的奖励黑客机会直接嵌入到环境中。这使得对这类机会的利用在设计中可验证，从而能够确定性地、自动地测量智能体是否以及如何利用此类漏洞。我们将该方法实例化为TextArena，并发布了Hack-Verifiable TextArena，这是一个可可靠测量奖励黑客行为的测试平台。利用这一基准，我们在多种环境和设置下分析了语言模型中的奖励黑客行为。我们已在https://github.com/MajoRoth/hack-verifiable-environments/开源了代码。

Original abstract: Aligning autonomous agents with human intent remains a central challenge in modern AI. A key manifestation of this challenge is reward hacking, whereby agents appear successful under the evaluation signal while violating the intended objective. Reward hacking has been observed across a wide range of settings, yet methods for reliably measuring it at scale remain lacking. In this work, we introduce a new evaluation paradigm for measuring reward hacking. Whereas prior studies have primarily analyzed it post hoc by inspecting agent trajectories, we instead embed detectable reward hacking opportunities directly into environments. This makes their exploitation verifiable by design, enabling deterministic and automated measurement of whether and how agents exploit such vulnerabilities. We instantiate this approach in $\textit{TextArena}$ and release $\textit{Hack-Verifiable TextArena}$, a testbed in which reward hacking can be measured reliably. Using this benchmark, we analyze reward hacking behavior across language models in diverse environments and settings. We open source the code at https://github.com/MajoRoth/hack-verifiable-environments/.

</details>


### [73] [The Hidden Signal of Verifier Strictness: Controlling and Improving Step-Wise Verification via Selective Latent Steering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20745v1)
*Yefan Zhou,Yilun Zhou,Austin Xu,Soroush Vosoughi,Shafiq Joty,Jiang Gui*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 控制验证器严格性的隐状态干预方法，可迁移至coding agent步骤验证

TL;DR: 提出VerifySteer，通过隐藏状态干预控制生成式验证器的严格度，无需微调，在错误检测和正确性认证间取得平衡，性能优于基线且计算高效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式验证器在逐步验证中校准不佳，容易过于宽松或严格，需要一种无需微调的控制方法。

Method: 发现验证器倾向编码在段落边界，利用隐藏状态引导调节严格度，并提出VerifySteer通过样本级路由和选择性干预平衡错误检测与正确性认证。

Result: 在ProcessBench和Hard2Verify上优于提示优化和激活引导基线，与自一致性方法竞争力相当且推理计算量减少4-7倍，可与微调互补。

Conclusion: 隐藏状态引导可有效控制验证器严格度，VerifySteer是一种高效且互补的方法，适用于生成式验证器校准。

中文摘要：生成式验证器已成为逐步验证的一种有前景的范式，但其验证行为往往校准不佳：它们可能过于宽松而遗漏错误步骤，或过于严格而拒绝正确的推理。我们将这种过度宽容或过度严格的倾向称为验证器严格度。在这项工作中，我们研究是否可以通过隐藏状态干预来控制验证器严格度。我们发现了一个特定于验证的隐藏状态信号：在逐步验证中，验证器接受或拒绝某个解决方案步骤的倾向编码在相应验证段落的边界附近。利用这一信号，我们展示了隐藏状态引导可以直接调节验证器严格度而无需微调。然而，统一引导会在错误检测与正确性认证之间引入权衡。为解决这一问题，我们提出了VerifySteer，它利用潜在的正确性信号进行样本级路由，并选择性地干预段落边界。在ProcessBench和Hard2Verify上的实验表明，VerifySteer优于提示优化和激活引导基线，并且与自一致性方法相比具有竞争力，同时推理计算量减少4-7倍。VerifySteer还可以与验证微调互补，在微调验证器的基础上进一步提升性能。代码可在https://github.com/YefanZhou/VerifySteer获取。

Original abstract: Generative verifiers have emerged as a promising paradigm for step-wise verification, but their verification behavior is often poorly calibrated: they may be under-critical and miss erroneous steps, or over-critical and reject correct reasoning. We refer to this tendency to be overly lenient or overly critical as verifier strictness. In this work, we study whether verifier strictness can be controlled through hidden-state intervention. We uncover a verification-specific hidden-state signal: in step-wise verification, a verifier's tendency to accept or reject a solution step is encoded near the boundary of the corresponding verification paragraph. Exploiting this signal, we show that hidden-state steering can directly modulate verifier strictness without fine-tuning. However, uniform steering induces a trade-off between error detection and correctness certification. To address this, we propose VerifySteer, which exploits latent correctness signals for sample-level routing and selectively intervenes on paragraph boundaries. Experiments on ProcessBench and Hard2Verify show that VerifySteer outperforms prompt optimization and activation steering baselines, and is competitive with self-consistency while requiring 4-7x less inference compute. VerifySteer is also complementary to verification fine-tuning, providing further gains on top of fine-tuned verifiers. The code is available at https://github.com/YefanZhou/VerifySteer.

</details>


### [74] [The Constraint Tax: Measuring Validity-Correctness Tradeoffs in Structured Outputs for Small Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26128v1)
*Jaideep Ray*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对小型语言模型施加硬性输出约束会显著降低答案准确率并引入约束税，建议采用延迟约束（自由推理，晚约束）的设计模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通常的工程假设认为硬输出约束能提高可靠性而不改变底层答案，但该假设可能不适用于小模型。本文旨在量化这种假设在小模型上的风险，并揭示结构化输出约束带来的准确率损失。

Method: 引入约束税（constraint tax）测量协议，通过在固定模型、任务分布和问题实例下隔离约束导致的答案准确率与可执行准确率损失，并在Qwen2.5-0.5B、Qwen2.5-1.5B和SmolLM2-1.7B三个小模型上进行15000次商品GPU生成实验，对比硬模式解码与提示仅JSON的效果。

Result: 硬答案模式解码使模式有效性从61.5%升至100.0%，但答案准确率从19.7%降至11.0%，错误有效模式输出从49.5%增至88.9%。在日历工具调用任务中，可执行准确率从91.5%（仅提示JSON）降至48.0%（硬工具调用模式），且两种模式均100%符合模式。错误是语义性的而非结构性的。3B边界模型仍存在直接模式税。

Conclusion: 小模型上硬输出约束有害，延迟包装（自由推理，晚约束）是一种更优的设计模式。生产系统应分别报告模式有效性、答案准确率、可执行准确率和错误有效模式率，以全面评估约束影响。

中文摘要：生产级LLM系统越来越需要机器可读的输出：JSON对象、类型化轨迹、正则约束字段和工具调用模式。本文针对设备端和低成本的小语言模型（SLM）部署，其中低于3B参数的模型在隐私、延迟和商品硬件方面具有吸引力，但在满足模式的同时解决问题的能力有限。通常的工程假设是硬输出约束能够提高可靠性而不改变底层答案。我们证明这一假设对于小模型是不安全的。我们引入了“约束税”，一种测量协议，用于在固定模型、固定任务分布和固定问题实例下隔离由结构化输出约束引起的答案和可执行准确率损失。在使用Qwen2.5-0.5B、Qwen2.5-1.5B和SmolLM2-1.7B进行的15000次商品GPU生成中，硬答案模式解码将模式有效性从61.5%提高到100.0%，但答案准确率从19.7%降低到11.0%，并且错误有效模式输出从49.5%增加到88.9%。最强行业类比是一个确定性日历工具调用任务：Qwen2.5-1.5B在仅提示JSON时达到91.5%的可执行准确率，但在相同硬工具调用模式下仅为48.0%，而两种模式都100%符合模式。错误是语义的，而非结构的。我们还表明，3B边界仍然支付直接模式税，并且延迟包装支持一种建设性的设计模式：自由推理，晚约束。实际结论直接：生产系统应分别报告模式有效性、答案准确率、可执行准确率和错误有效模式率。

Original abstract: Production LLM systems increasingly require machine-readable outputs: JSON objects, typed traces, regex-constrained fields, and tool-call schemas. This paper targets on-device and low-cost small language model (SLM) deployments, where sub-3B models are attractive for privacy, latency, and commodity hardware but have limited capacity to satisfy schemas while solving tasks. The usual engineering assumption is that hard output constraints improve reliability without changing the underlying answer. We show that this assumption is unsafe for small models. We introduce \emph{constraint tax}, a measurement protocol for isolating the answer and executable-accuracy loss caused by structured-output constraints at fixed model, fixed task distribution, and fixed problem instances. Across 15,000 commodity-GPU generations with Qwen2.5-0.5B, Qwen2.5-1.5B, and SmolLM2-1.7B, hard answer-only schema decoding raises schema validity from 61.5\% to 100.0\%, but lowers answer accuracy from 19.7\% to 11.0\% and increases wrong-valid-schema outputs from 49.5\% to 88.9\%. The strongest industry analogue is a deterministic calendar tool-call task: Qwen2.5-1.5B achieves 91.5\% executable accuracy with prompt-only JSON but only 48.0\% under the same hard tool-call schema, while both modes are 100.0\% schema-valid. The error is semantic, not structural. We also show that the 3B boundary still pays a direct-schema tax and that delayed packaging supports a constructive design pattern: reason free, constrain late. The practical conclusion is direct: production systems should report schema validity, answer accuracy, executable accuracy, and wrong-valid-schema rate separately.

</details>


### [75] [Multi-Step Likelihood-Ratio Correction for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20865v1)
*Deokgyu Yoon,Hyungkyu Kang,Joongkyu Lee,Byeongchan Kim,Gyungin Shin,Sungrae Park,Min-hwan Oh*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多步似然比校正的RLVR算法，可直接用于coding agent的RL训练

TL;DR: 提出N步前向迹策略优化（NFPO），通过引入累积似然比改进PPO代理目标，在偏差-方差权衡中提供连续桥接，理论证明更紧的策略改进界，实验验证推理性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PPO代理目标因局部近似引入结构性偏差，需信任区域控制，现有方法不能有效管理偏差-方差权衡。

Method: 引入N步前向迹，利用未来N-1个令牌的累积似然比增强PPO代理目标，并将其集成到掩码策略梯度框架中，形成NFPO算法。

Result: 理论分析表明NFPO目标比标准PPO有更紧的策略改进界；在多个推理基准上实验显示一致性能提升。

Conclusion: NFPO为控制偏差-方差权衡提供了原则性机制，有效提升大语言模型推理能力。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在提升大语言模型推理能力方面发挥着关键作用。然而，广泛使用的PPO代理目标本质上是局部性的，因为它们依赖于精确策略梯度目标的局部近似。虽然这种近似通过降低重要性采样引起的方差提高了稳定性，但它也在代理目标中引入了结构性偏差，必须通过信任区域机制加以控制。在这项工作中，我们引入了N步前向迹，利用接下来N-1个令牌的累积似然比来增强PPO代理目标。基于这一思想，我们提出了N步前向迹策略优化（NFPO），一种将N步前向迹集成到掩码策略梯度框架中的实用RLVR算法。NFPO在PPO代理目标和精确策略梯度目标之间提供了一个连续的桥梁，为控制偏差-方差权衡提供了一种原则性机制。我们的理论分析表明，通过适当选择N，所提出的目标比标准PPO代理产生更紧的策略改进界。在全面推理基准上的实验表明，NFPO持续改进性能，支持了我们的理论发现。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) plays a pivotal role in improving the reasoning ability of large language models. However, widely used PPO surrogate objectives are fundamentally local, as they rely on a local approximation of the exact policy gradient objective. While this approximation improves stability by reducing the variance induced by importance sampling, it also introduces structural bias into the surrogate objective, which must be controlled through trust region mechanisms. In this work, we introduce the $N$-step forward trace, which augments the PPO surrogate objective using the cumulative likelihood ratio of the next $N-1$ tokens. Building on this idea, we propose $N$-Step Forward-Trace Policy Optimization (NFPO), a practical RLVR algorithm that integrates the $N$-step forward trace into the masked policy gradient framework. NFPO provides a continuous bridge between the PPO surrogate objective and the exact policy gradient objective, offering a principled mechanism for controlling the bias-variance trade-off. Our theoretical analysis shows that, with an appropriate choice of $N$, the proposed objective yields a tighter policy-improvement bound than the standard PPO surrogate. Experiments on comprehensive reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that NFPO consistently improves performance, supporting our theoretical findings.

</details>


### [76] [Domain-Adaptable Reinforcement Learning for Code Generation with Dense Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21180v1)
*Erfan Aghadavoodi Jolfaei,Daniel Maninger,Abhinav Anand,Mert Tiftikci,Mira Mezini*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在自动代码生成中缺乏对正确性、质量、安全性和领域约束的保证，尤其在机器人领域需考虑环境与物理约束。

Method: 使用近端策略优化（PPO）微调预训练LLMs，设计可执行感知奖励公式（覆盖语法、功能正确性、风格、安全性、模拟器可执行性），并采用令牌级奖励映射机制实现从执行结果到生成令牌的信用分配。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在自动代码生成方面展现出强大的潜力，但缺乏对正确性、质量、安全性和领域特定约束的保证。例如在机器人领域，代码生成正越来越多地用于规划和执行动作，对环境和物理约束的意识至关重要。为了促进代码生成的LLMs适应包括领域特定要求在内的多样化需求，我们提出了一个强化学习框架，使用近端策略优化对预训练的LLMs进行微调。我们定制的可执行感知奖励公式捕获并优化语法、功能正确性、代码风格、安全性和模拟器可执行性。一种令牌级奖励映射机制使得从执行结果到生成令牌的有效信用分配成为可能。该框架在通用代码生成（MBPP/MBPP+）和机器人程序合成（RoboEval）上进行了评估。结果表明功能正确性和模拟器可执行性有显著改进，包括在MBPP上绝对pass@1提高了19%，在RoboEval上执行故障减少了51%。这些发现表明，结构化强化学习可以有效地将语言模型与正确的程序生成和领域特定要求对齐。

Original abstract: Large language models show strong potential for automated code generation, but lack guarantees for correctness, quality, safety, and domain-specific constraints. For instance in robotics, where code generation is increasingly being used for planning and executing actions, awareness of the environment and physical constraints is critical. To facilitate the adaption of code-generating LLMs to diverse requirements, including domain-specific ones, we present a reinforcement learning framework that fine-tunes pre-trained LLMs using proximal policy optimization. Our customizable execution-aware reward formula captures and optimizes syntax, functional correctness, code style, security, and simulator executability. A token-level reward mapping mechanism enables effective credit assignment from execution outcomes to generated tokens. The framework is evaluated on general-purpose code generation (MBPP/MBPP+) and robotic program synthesis (RoboEval). The results show substantial improvements in functional correctness and simulator executability, including an absolute pass@1 increase of 19% on MBPP and a reduction in execution failures by 51% on RoboEval. These findings demonstrate that structured reinforcement learning can effectively align language models to correct program generation and domain-specific requirements.

### [77] [APEX: Autonomous Policy Exploration for Self-Evolving LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21240v1)
*Yibo Li,Jiashuo Yang,Zhi Zheng,Zhiyuan Hu,Yuan Sui,Shizun Wang,Yufei He,Bryan Hooi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 直接研究自演化LLM agent的探索与策略规划，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: APEX通过构建策略图（有向无环图）并设计分支发现和策略选择机制，解决了自进化LLM代理中的探索崩溃问题，在多个基准上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自进化代理在测试时通过记忆和反思学习，但容易因探索崩溃（即行为集中于已知高奖励策略）而错过更好的替代方案，需要一种方法在积累经验的同时维持探索能力。

Method: 提出APEX框架，包含一个策略图（有向无环图的里程碑和依赖关系），通过分支发现（Fork Discovery）基于证据扩展新方向，并通过策略选择（Policy Selection）在规划时平衡探索与利用。

Result: 在九个Jericho文字冒险游戏和WebArena基准上，APEX优于所有基线，消融实验证实各组件有效且鲁棒。

Conclusion: APEX通过显式策略空间和平衡探索-利用的机制，有效实现了自进化代理中的持续探索，提升了复杂任务中的性能。

中文摘要：LLM代理在一系列复杂的任务中表现出色，包括需要长期决策的交互环境。但这些代理在测试时无法即时学习。自进化代理通过跨情节积累记忆和反思来解决这一问题，而无需更新模型权重。然而，这些代理常常遭受探索崩溃：随着记忆增长，行为集中在熟悉的、高奖励的常规上，减少了发现更好替代方案的机会。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了自主策略探索（APEX），它通过策略图——一个有向无环图，包含具有先决依赖关系的里程碑——构建并维护一个显式策略空间。在APEX中，分支发现通过有证据支持的未探索方向扩展图，而策略选择在规划过程中平衡探索与利用。在九个Jericho文字冒险游戏和WebArena（一个真实的网络交互基准）上的评估中，APEX优于所有基线。广泛的消融实验验证了每个组件的贡献，并展示了在不同设置下的鲁棒性，证明了APEX在自进化代理中实现持续探索的有效性。

Original abstract: LLM agents have shown strong performance across a wide range of complex tasks, including interactive environments that require long-horizon decision making. But these agents cannot learn on the fly at test time. Self-evolving agents address this by accumulating memory and reflection across episodes rather than requiring model-weight updates. However, these agents often suffer from exploration collapse: as memory grows, behavior concentrates around familiar high-reward routines, reducing the chance of discovering better alternatives. To address this problem, we propose Autonomous Policy EXploration (APEX), which builds and maintains an explicit strategy space through a strategy map-a directed acyclic graph of milestones with prerequisite dependency edges. In APEX, Fork Discovery expands the map with evidence-grounded unexplored directions, while Policy Selection balances exploration and exploitation during planning. Evaluated on nine Jericho text-adventure games and WebArena, a realistic web interaction benchmark, APEX outperforms all baselines. Extensive ablations validate each component's contribution and demonstrate robustness across diverse settings, demonstrating APEX's effectiveness for sustained exploration in self-evolving agents.

### [78] [FedCritic: Serverless Federated Critic Learning-based Resource Allocation for Multi-Cell OFDMA in 6G](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21418v1)
*Amin Farajzadeh,Melike Erol-Kantarci*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FedCritic，一种用于6G超密集网络的去中心化资源管理框架，通过联邦评论家实现稳定训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 6G超密集网络中干扰耦合严重，需要分布式解决方案满足QoS约束。

Method: 基于多智能体演员-评论家，通过八卦协议联邦化评论家参数，去中心化执行。

Result: 在复用-1场景中，FedCritic相比基线提高了SINR、小区边缘速率、总速率和公平性，训练更稳定。

Conclusion: FedCritic有效解决了分布式资源管理问题，降低了协调开销。

中文摘要：在第六代（6G）超密集网络中，激进的频率复用放大了小区间干扰（ICI），使得多小区正交频分多址（OFDMA）调度和功率控制跨相邻小区强耦合。我们研究在干扰耦合和长期每用户服务质量（QoS）最小速率约束下的分布式下行链路资源管理——联合子载波调度和功率分配。通过使用虚拟队列赤字权重来强制执行长期QoS，我们提出了FedCritic，一种具有去中心化执行的无服务器联邦多智能体演员-评论家框架。与需要集中式评论家学习和联合轨迹聚合的集中训练去中心化执行（CTDE）方法不同，FedCritic通过在干扰图上进行轻量级的基于八卦的参数平均来联邦化评论家，实现了在没有中央协调器的情况下稳定的价值估计，同时保持策略本地化。在干扰严重的复用-1设置中的模拟表明，相对于非协调和CTDE基线，FedCritic提高了平均信干噪比（SINR）和小区边缘速率，增加了网络范围的平均总速率和公平性，并且实现了更稳定的训练和更低的协调开销。

Original abstract: In sixth-generation (6G) ultra-dense networks, aggressive frequency reuse amplifies inter-cell interference (ICI), making multi-cell orthogonal frequency-division multiple access (OFDMA) scheduling and power control strongly coupled across neighboring cells. We study distributed downlink resource management -- joint subcarrier scheduling and power allocation -- under interference coupling and long-term per-user quality-of-service (QoS) minimum-rate constraints. By using virtual-queue deficit weights to enforce long-term QoS, we develop FedCritic, a serverless federated multi-agent actor-critic framework with decentralized execution. Unlike centralized training with decentralized execution (CTDE) approaches that require centralized critic learning and joint trajectory aggregation, FedCritic federates the critic through lightweight gossip-based parameter averaging over the interference graph, enabling stable value estimation without a central coordinator while keeping policies local. Simulations in an interference-rich reuse-1 setting show that FedCritic improves mean signal-to-interference-plus-noise ratio (SINR) and cell-edge rate, increases network-wide average sum-rate and fairness relative to non-coordinated and CTDE baselines, and achieves more stable training with lower coordination overhead.

</details>


### [79] [Agent JIT Compilation for Latency-Optimizing Web Agent Planning and Scheduling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21470v2)
*Caleb Winston,Ron Yifeng Wang,Azalia Mirhoseini,Christos Kozyrakis*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: Agent JIT编译，将任务编译为代码并并行化，直接提升web agent性能，与代码优化相关。

TL;DR: 提出智能体即时编译系统，通过编译任务描述为可执行代码，结合代码计划生成、并行化调度和工具协议，显著加速计算机使用智能体并提高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前计算机使用智能体采用顺序循环架构，导致高延迟和频繁错误，亟需更高效的执行方式。

Method: 提出JIT编译系统，包含JIT-Planner（生成并验证代码计划）、JIT-Scheduler（蒙特卡洛成本估计探索并行化）和不变性强制工具协议（减少错误工具使用）。

Result: 在五个应用中，JIT-Planner比Browser-Use加速10.4倍且准确率提高28%，JIT-Scheduler比OpenAI CUA加速2.4倍且准确率提高9%。

Conclusion: JIT编译系统通过并行化和协议约束有效降低了延迟和错误，提升了计算机使用智能体的性能。

中文摘要：计算机使用智能体（CUAs）通过生成对工具（如点击、键入和滚动浏览器）的调用序列，来自动化以自然语言指定的任务，例如“从Taco Bell订购最便宜的商品”。当前的实现遵循顺序的获取屏幕截图-执行循环，其中每次迭代都需要一次LLM调用，导致高延迟和因不正确的工具使用而频繁出错。我们提出了智能体即时（JIT）编译系统，该系统将任务描述直接编译为可执行代码，其中可能包括LLM调用、工具调用和并行化。我们的方法包括三个组成部分：（1）JIT-Planner，它生成多个代码计划，根据工具规范验证每个计划，并选择成本最低的候选计划；（2）JIT-Scheduler，它通过从学习到的延迟分布中进行蒙特卡洛成本估计来探索并行化策略；以及（3）一个不变性强制工具协议，指定前置条件和后置条件要求，以减少不正确工具使用的比率。在五个应用中，JIT-Planner比Browser-Use实现了10.4倍的加速和28%的更高准确率，而JIT-Scheduler比OpenAI CUA实现了2.4倍的加速和9%的更高准确率。

Original abstract: Computer-use agents (CUAs) automate tasks specified with natural language such as "order the cheapest item from Taco Bell" by generating sequences of calls to tools such as click, type, and scroll on a browser. Current implementations follow a sequential fetch-screenshot-execute loop where each iteration requires an LLM call, resulting in high latency and frequent errors from incorrect tool use. We present agent just-in-time (JIT) compilation, a system that compiles task descriptions directly into executable code that may include LLM calls, tool calls, and parallelization. Our approach comprises three components: (1) JIT-Planner, which generates multiple code plans, validates each against tool specifications, and selects the minimum-cost candidate; (2) JIT-Scheduler, which explores parallelization strategies via Monte Carlo cost estimation from learned latency distributions; and (3) an invariant-enforcing tool protocol specifying precondition and postcondition requirements to reduce the rate of incorrect tool use. Across five applications, JIT-Planner achieves $10.4\times$ speedup and 28$\%$ higher accuracy over Browser-Use, while JIT-Scheduler achieves $2.4\times$ speedup and 9\% higher accuracy over OpenAI CUA.

### [80] [When Are Teacher Tokens Reliable? Position-Weighted On-Policy Self-Distillation for Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21606v1)
*Xiaogeng Liu,Xinyan Wang,Yingzi Ma,Yechao Zhang,Chaowei Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 推理自蒸馏中教师token可靠性分析，可视为agent自我改进方法，边界保留。

TL;DR: 提出位置加权策略自蒸馏，利用轨迹级位置分数预测教师令牌可靠性，提升推理蒸馏效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准OPSD平等对待所有令牌，但教师令牌可靠性在不同位置差异大，现有熵方法无法区分不确定性与多样性。

Method: 引入分支可行性诊断，发现位置分数优于局部不确定性；提出PW-OPSD，在保持OPSD框架下对令牌加权递增位置权重。

Result: 在AIME 2024/2025上Avg@12提升1.0/1.1点，在更大模型上也有泛化改进。

Conclusion: 推理蒸馏中教师令牌可靠性具有轨迹结构，可通过位置加权利用，无需额外教师计算。

中文摘要：在策略自蒸馏（OPSD）利用特权教师在其自身轨迹上训练学生，但其标准目标对所有生成的令牌一视同仁，隐式地将特权教师目标视为在每个学生访问的前缀上同样可靠。现有的基于熵的OPD方法通过用教师熵调节令牌级监督来放松这种均匀性，但在推理中，高教师熵具有模糊的可靠性含义：它既可以反映不可行的不确定性，也可以反映良性的解决方案多样性。为了识别这一现象，我们引入了分支可行性诊断。具体来说，我们记录来自特权答案教师提示的下一个令牌替代方案，在学生提示加上其策略骨干前缀后强制每个替代方案，并测试生成的学生模板续写是否恢复正确答案。在Qwen3-4B上，我们发现定向的序列内位置分数是教师令牌可靠性的最强预测指标，达到0.83的ROC曲线下面积（AUROC）；局部不确定性分数最多为0.57。受这种轨迹级结构的启发，我们提出了位置加权策略自蒸馏（PW-OPSD），它在保持与学生轨迹、特权教师传递和截断前向KL目标相同的情况下，应用递增的位置权重。在我们使用不同随机种子的综合评估中，基于诊断的PW-OPSD在AIME 2024和AIME 2025的Avg@12上分别提高了+1.0和+1.1个百分点，并且在来自不同家族的两个更大规模模型（DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B和Olmo-3-7B-Think）上的泛化评估也显示出一致的Avg@12总体改进。这些结果表明，推理蒸馏中教师令牌的可靠性是轨迹结构化的，并且可以在不增加教师计算的情况下加以利用。

Original abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) trains a student on its own rollouts using a privileged teacher, but its standard objective weights all generated tokens equally, implicitly treating the privileged teacher target as equally reliable at every student-visited prefix. Existing entropy-based OPD methods relax this uniformity by modulating token-level supervision with teacher entropy, but high teacher entropy in reasoning has an ambiguous reliability meaning: it can reflect either non-viable uncertainty or benign solution diversity. To identify this phenomenon, we introduce a branch-viability diagnostic. Specifically, we record next-token alternatives from the privileged-answer teacher prompt, force each alternative after the student prompt plus its on-policy spine prefix, and test whether the resulting student-template continuation recovers the correct answer. On Qwen3-4B, we find that an oriented within-sequence position score is the strongest tested predictor of teacher-token reliability, reaching an area-under-ROC-curve (AUROC) of 0.83; local uncertainty scores are at most 0.57. Motivated by this trajectory-level structure, we propose Position-Weighted On-Policy Self-Distillation (PW-OPSD), which applies an increasing position weight while keeping the same student rollout, privileged teacher pass, and clipped forward-KL target as OPSD. In our comprehensive evaluations with different random seeds, the diagnostic-derived PW-OPSD improves AIME 2024 and AIME 2025 Avg@12 by +1.0 and +1.1 points, and a generalization evaluation on two larger-scale models from different families, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B and Olmo-3-7B-Think, also demonstrates consistent aggregate Avg@12 improvements. These results show that teacher-token reliability in reasoning distillation is trajectory-structured and can be utilized without additional teacher computation.

</details>


### [81] [Value-Gradient Hypothesis of RL for LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21654v1)
*Arip Asadulaev,Daniil Ognev,Karim Salta,Martin Takac*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL for LLMs价值梯度分析，涉及PPO/GRPO训练机制，可迁移到agent训练。

TL;DR: 从价值梯度视角解释无批评家强化学习在LLM后训练中的有效性，并给出RL影响最大的时机判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无批评家RL方法（如PPO和GRPO）在LLM后训练中表现优异但理论理解不足，需要解释其为何有效以及何时能带来最大改进。

Method: 通过可微分轨迹展开和加性噪声参数化，证明actor更新在期望上等于价值梯度；对离散Transformer策略，分析自动微分通过注意力机制产生的经验成本状态近似价值信号，并分解RL影响为价值梯度信号和可达奖励余量。

Result: 发现actor更新具有价值梯度性质，自动微分产生的经验成本状态逼近价值信号，误差受采样间隔和策略熵控制；RL影响可分解为价值梯度信号和可达奖励余量。

Conclusion: 该视角为无批评家RL在LLM后训练中的有效性和增益时机提供了理论依据，并给出了沿预训练轨迹RL最有效的判据。

中文摘要：强化学习显著改善了预训练语言模型，但为什么无评论家方法（如PPO和GRPO）如此有效以及何时能提供最大增益仍未得到充分研究。我们为LLM后训练中的无评论家RL开发了一个价值梯度视角。首先，在可微分轨迹展开和加性噪声参数化下，我们表明演员更新在期望上类似于价值梯度：反向传播传播成本状态，其条件期望等于价值梯度。其次，对于离散Transformer策略，我们表明通过注意力机制的自动微分产生的经验成本状态近似于这一价值信号，其误差由采样间隔和策略熵控制。这些结果将RL的影响分解为价值梯度信号和可达奖励余量，从而得出了在预训练轨迹上RL何时最有效的判断标准。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning substantially improves pretrained language models, but it remains understudied why critic-free methods such as PPO and GRPO work as well as they do, and when they should provide the largest gains. We develop a value-gradient perspective of critic-free RL for LLM post-training. First, under a differentiable rollout and additive-noise parameterization, we show that the actor update is value-gradient-like in expectation: the backward pass propagates costates whose conditional expectation equals the value gradient. Second, for discrete transformer policies, we show that autodifferentiation through attention produces empirical costates that approximate this value signal, with an error controlled by the sampling gap and policy entropy. These results motivate a decomposition of RL impact into value gradient signal and reachable reward headroom, yielding a criterion for when RL should be most effective along a pretraining trajectory.

</details>

### [82] [Decoupling Communication from Policy: Robust MARL under Bandwidth Constraints](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21085v1)
*Alexi Canesse,Benoît Goupil,Jesse Read,Sonia Vanier*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent强化学习通信解耦，涉及多agent协作

TL;DR: 提出归一化带宽预算β和解耦通信与策略表示的SLIM架构，在带宽受限的MARL中实现最先进性能并保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MARL通信架构中，共享潜在表示同时用于策略执行和通信，导致减少消息大小直接限制策略容量，性能严重下降。

Method: 提出归一化带宽预算β统一稀疏性、轮次和消息维度；设计SLIM架构解耦通信路径与策略潜在表示，实现同步通信并隔离带宽影响。

Result: 在多个部分可观测MARL基准测试中，SLIM达到最先进性能，带宽减少时仅轻微性能下降，展现可扩展性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过解耦通信与策略表示，可以在限制带宽时保持高性能，为带宽受限的MARL应用提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：通信在多智能体强化学习（MARL）中能够实现协调，但许多现实应用（例如，使用无人机群进行搜索与救援）在严格的带宽约束下运行。许多通信架构仍然存在一个耦合的瓶颈：共享的潜在表示同时用于策略执行和智能体间通信。因此，减少消息大小直接限制了策略的潜在空间，通常导致显著的性能下降。我们通过两个贡献来解决这个问题。首先，我们引入了β，一个归一化的每智能体带宽预算，将稀疏性、轮次和消息维度统一为一个可比较的约束。其次，我们提供了SLIM，一种最小架构，将通信路径与策略的潜在表示解耦，使我们能够在隔离带宽对策略容量的影响的同时，受益于同步通信。我们在几个部分可观测的MARL基准测试上评估了我们的方法，这些基准测试中通信至关重要。我们的方法实现了最先进的性能，并在有限通信下表现出可扩展性和鲁棒性，随着带宽的减少只有轻微的性能下降。

Original abstract: Communication enables coordination in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), but many real-world applications, e.g., search-and-rescue with drone swarms, operate under severe bandwidth constraints. Many communication architectures still expose a coupled bottleneck in which a shared latent representation is used for both policy execution and inter-agent communication. Consequently, reducing message size directly limits the policy's latent space, often leading to significant performance degradation. We address this with two contributions. First, we introduce $β$, a normalised per-agent bandwidth budget that unifies sparsity, rounds, and message dimension into a single comparable constraint. Second, we provide SLIM, a minimal architecture that decouples the communication pathway from the policy's latent representation, allowing us to isolate the effect of bandwidth from the effect of policy capacity while benefiting from in-step communication. We evaluate our method on several partially-observable MARL benchmarks, where communication is essential. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance and exhibits scalability and robustness under limited communication, with only marginal degradation as bandwidth is reduced.

</details>

### [83] [Causal Past Logic for Runtime Verification of Distributed LLM Agent Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20923v1)
*Benedikt Bollig*

Main category: cs.LO

Selection reason: 为分布式LLM agent工作流提出因果逻辑运行时验证，对agent可靠性和验证有可迁移价值。

TL;DR: 提出因果过去逻辑（CPL）用于分布式LLM代理工作流中的运行时监控，使验证成为协调语言的一部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式异步执行中，传统基于顺序日志的监控方式不适用，因为事件因果可见性差异导致局部决策可能基于未知信息。

Method: 扩展ZipperGen框架，集成CPL作为守卫的源级逻辑，使用向量时钟监视器在线评估，并证明与指称语义一致。

Result: 实现了运行时验证嵌入协调语言，避免了事后日志检查。

Conclusion: 通过CPL，运行时验证成为协调语言的内置特性，提高了分布式代理工作流的监控准确性和实时性。

中文摘要：分布式LLM代理工作流不应被监控，如同它们产生单一的连续日志。在异步执行中，决策只能依赖于因果上对做出决策的生命线可见的事件：某个日志中较早出现的事件可能仍然在局部未知。我们将ZipperGen代理工作流框架扩展为包含因果过去逻辑（CPL），这是一种用于条件语句和while循环中的守卫的小型过去时态逻辑。除了标准的过去时态模态（如前驱和持续）之外，守卫还可以检查另一生命线的最新因果可见事件以及其中存储的选定变量。该公式是一个源代码级别的守卫：由所属生命线在线评估，并能在运行时影响控制流。我们给出了一个具有最新值视图的向量时钟监视器，并证明了本地计算的监视器值与当前事件下守卫的指称语义一致。因此，运行时验证成为协调语言本身的一部分，而不是对执行日志的事后检查。

Original abstract: Distributed LLM agent workflows should not be monitored as if they produced a single sequential log. In an asynchronous execution, a decision can only depend on events that are causally visible to the lifeline that makes it: an event that appears earlier in some log may still be unknown locally. We extend the ZipperGen agent-workflow framework with Causal Past Logic (CPL), a small past-time temporal logic for guards in conditionals and while loops. In addition to standard past-time modalities such as previous and since, a guard can inspect the latest causally visible event of another lifeline and selected variables stored there. The formula is a source-level guard: it is evaluated online by the owner lifeline and can influence control flow at runtime. We give a vector-clock monitor with latest-value views and prove that the locally computed monitor value coincides with the denotational semantics of the guard at the current event. Thus runtime verification becomes part of the coordination language itself, rather than a post-hoc check over an execution log.

</details>

### [84] [Frontier: Towards Comprehensive and Accurate LLM Inference Simulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21312v2)
*Yicheng Feng,Xin Tan,Yangtao Deng,Yimin Jiang,Yibo Zhu,Hong Xu*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: LLM推理模拟器支持agentic调度，可迁移至coding agent部署验证。

TL;DR: 提出了Frontier，一个用于现代LLM推理服务的离散事件模拟器，采用解耦抽象，准确模拟性能，在16 H800上吞吐量误差低于4%，延迟误差大幅降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM服务模拟器缺乏架构完整性和决策级保真度，不适用于解耦服务和复杂优化场景，导致预测失真。

Method: Frontier采用解耦抽象，建模共置、PDD和AFD等结构，在调度器-批处理引擎循环中集成运行时优化（如CUDA Graphs、投机解码），支持有状态请求，并提供准确的计算、通信和内存成本预测。

Result: 在16 H800 GPU测试平台上，平均吞吐量误差低于4%；端到端延迟误差在共置下从44.9%降至6.4%，在解耦下从51.7%降至2.6%；可扩展至1000+ GPU。

Conclusion: Frontier能有效模拟现代LLM服务，支持SLA帕累托前沿探索、异构解耦分配等新用例，并已开源。

中文摘要：现代LLM服务不再是同质或单一的。生产系统现在结合了解耦执行、复杂并行化、运行时优化以及有状态工作负载，如推理、智能体和强化学习展开。模拟对于探索这个不断增长的设计空间很有吸引力，然而现有的模拟器缺乏其所需的架构完整性和决策级保真度。它们的单体副本抽象不适用于解耦服务，而平均情况的分析代理会扭曲SLA预测甚至颠倒优化结论。我们提出了Frontier，一个用于现代LLM推理服务的离散事件模拟器。Frontier具有解耦抽象。它通过建模共置、预填充-解码解耦（PDD）和注意力-FFN解耦（AFD）以及具有特定角色的集群工作者，捕获了现代服务系统的结构和动态，在调度器-批处理引擎循环中融入了关键运行时优化（例如，CUDA Graphs、投机解码），并支持新兴工作负载的有状态请求。它还提供了跨多样化服务场景和复杂工作负载组合的准确且可推广的计算、通信和内存成本预测。在16块H800 GPU测试平台上，Frontier实现了平均吞吐量误差低于4%。与最先进的模拟器相比，它在共置下将端到端延迟误差从44.9%降低到6.4%，在解耦下从51.7%降低到2.6%。它可在普通CPU上扩展到超过1000块GPU，并支持新的用例，如依赖SLA的帕累托前沿探索、异构解耦分配、智能体推理调度验证和强化学习后训练重配置。我们在https://github.com/NetX-lab/Frontier上发布Frontier。

Original abstract: Modern LLM serving is no longer homogeneous or monolithic. Production systems now combine disaggregated execution, complex parallelism, runtime optimizations, and stateful workloads such as reasoning, agents, and RL rollouts. Simulation is attractive for exploring this growing design space, yet existing simulators lack the architectural completeness and decision-grade fidelity it demands. Their monolithic-replica abstractions are ill-suited to disaggregated serving, while average-case analytical proxies can distort SLA predictions and even reverse optimization conclusions.
  We present Frontier, a discrete-event simulator for modern LLM inference serving. Frontier features a disaggregated abstraction. It captures the structure and dynamics of modern serving systems by modeling co-location, Prefill-Decode Disaggregation (PDD), and Attention-FFN Disaggregation (AFD) with role-specific cluster workers, incorporating key runtime optimizations (e.g., CUDA Graphs, speculative decoding) within the scheduler-batch-engine loop, and supporting stateful requests for emerging workloads. It further provides accurate and generalizable predictions of computation, communication, and memory costs across diverse serving scenarios with complex workload compositions. On 16-H800 GPU testbed, Frontier achieves an average throughput error below 4%. Compared with state-of-the-art simulators, it reduces end-to-end latency error from 44.9% to 6.4% under co-location and from 51.7% to 2.6% under disaggregation. It scales to over 1K GPUs on commodity CPUs and enables new use cases such as SLA-dependent Pareto frontier exploration, heterogeneous disaggregated allocation, agentic reasoning scheduling validation, and RL post-training reconfiguration. We release Frontier at https://github.com/NetX-lab/Frontier.

</details>


<div id='stat.ML'></div>

# stat.ML [[Back]](#toc)

### [85] [Scalable Reinforcement Learning via Adaptive Batch Scaling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21557v2)
*Jongchan Park*

Main category: stat.ML

Selection reason: RL自适应批大小，训练方法可迁移至agent训练

TL;DR: 提出自适应批量缩放（ABS）方法，通过动态调整批量大小以匹配RL训练中的非平稳性演变，实现早期可塑性与后期收敛的平衡，在ALE基准上取得优于传统大规模批量的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为大批量训练与RL不兼容，但观察到非平稳性随训练阶段变化，早期需要小批量保持可塑性，后期大批量有利于精确收敛，因此希望自适应地调整批量大小以兼顾两者。

Method: 提出行为发散度（Behavioral Divergence）指标，量化连续更新间动作层面的策略非平稳性，并根据该指标动态调整有效批量大小（批量大小与策略波动性成反比），集成于并行Q网络（PQN）算法中。

Result: 在ALE基准上，ABS方法使更大网络和更大批量的组合实现了最佳性能，打破了传统认知，验证了自适应批量控制的有效性。

Conclusion: 非平稳性是动态演变的而非固定属性，通过自适应批量控制可以解锁RL中此前被认为不可实现的大网络大批量缩放行为，兼顾早期可塑性与后期收敛精度。

中文摘要：传统观点认为，大批量训练与强化学习（RL）根本不相容——超过适度阈值后，由于数据分布固有的非平稳性，增加批量大小通常会导致收益递减或性能下降。我们通过观察发现，非平稳性并非RL的固定属性，而是在训练过程中演变的：早期阶段表现出快速的行为变化，需要小批量以保持可塑性，而后期阶段接近准平稳状态，大批量可实现精确收敛。受此观察启发，我们提出了自适应批量缩放（ABS），根据学习策略的稳定程度动态调整有效批量大小。ABS的核心是行为发散度（Behavioral Divergence），一种通过衡量连续更新之间的动作层面变化来量化策略非平稳性的新指标，我们据此将批量大小与策略波动性成反比缩放。与并行Q网络（PQN）算法集成，并在ALE基准上评估，ABS无缝协调了早期可塑性与后期稳定收敛。引人注目的是，与传统观点相反，我们的结果表明，更大网络和更大批量大小的组合实现了最佳性能——这种以前被认为在RL中无法实现的缩放行为，现在通过自适应批量控制被解锁。

Original abstract: Conventional wisdom holds that large-batch training is fundamentally incompatible with Reinforcement Learning (RL) - beyond a modest threshold, increasing batch sizes typically yields diminishing returns or performance degradation due to the inherent non-stationarity of the data distribution. We challenge this view by observing that non-stationarity is not a fixed property of RL, but evolves throughout training: early stages exhibit rapid behavioral shifts that demand small batches for plasticity, whereas late stages approach a quasi-stationary regime where large batches enable precise convergence. Motivated by this observation, we propose Adaptive Batch Scaling (ABS), that dynamically adjusts the effective batch size according to the stability of the learning policy. Central to ABS is Behavioral Divergence, a novel metric that quantifies policy non-stationarity by measuring action-level shifts between consecutive updates, which we use to scale batch size inversely to policy volatility. Integrated with the Parallelised Q-Network (PQN) algorithm and evaluated on the ALE benchmark, ABS seamlessly reconciles early-stage plasticity with late-stage stable convergence. Strikingly, contrary to conventional wisdom, our results reveal that the combination of larger networks and larger batch sizes achieves the best performance - a scaling behavior previously thought to be unattainable in RL, now unlocked through adaptive batch control.

</details>
